---
about_this_resource_text: "<p><strong>Description:</strong> What is the maximum number\
  \ of edges in a graph forbidding a cycle of length four? What about forbidding a\
  \ complete bipartite graph of a fixed size? Professor Zhao discusses the K\u0151\
  v\xE1ri\u2013S\xF3s\u2013Tur\xE1n theorem, which gives an upper bound. In the case\
  \ of 4-cycles, a matching algebraic construction of a C4-free graph is also demonstrated.</p>\r\
  \n<p><strong>Instructor:</strong> Yufei Zhao</p>"
course_id: 18-217-graph-theory-and-additive-combinatorics-fall-2019
